Question 163 of 210
Question ID: 651610
Which of the following is an input to the Manage Team process?
Top of Form
- **A Work performance reports**
- **B Work performance information**
- **C Work performance data**
- **D Change requests**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Manage Team is the process of tracking team member performance, providing feedback,
resolving issues, and managing changes to optimize project performance.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Manage Team is the process of tracking team member performance, providing feedback,
resolving issues, and managing team changes to optimize project performance. The Manage
Team process has the following six inputs:
● Project management plan (resource management plan)
● Project documents (issue log, lessons learned register, project team assignments, team charter)
● Work performance reports (results from schedule control, cost control, quality control, and
scope validation)

---

● Team performance assessments
● EEFs
● OPAs
Aim to understand the flow of work performance data, information, and reports. Work
performance data is an output of the Executing process, Direct and Manage Project Work.
Control Resources is one of the Monitoring and Controlling processes that analyze the data to
output work performance information. In turn, this information serves as an input to Monitor and
Control Project Work so that data analysis can produce work performance reports. These reports
feed into the Perform Integrated Change Control, Manage Team, Manage Communications, and
Monitor Risks processes.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Work performance reports**
Correct. The results from analyzing work performance information on schedule control,
cost control, quality control, and scope validation may be included in work performance
reports that serve as an input to the Manage Team process. These reports can help
determine future team resource requirements and influence the team’s decision making.
- **B Work performance information**
Incorrect. The Control Resources process takes work performance data from processes in
the Executing Process Group, and using several data analysis techniques, produces the
output of work performance information for the Monitor and Control Project Work process.
Work performance information is not an input to the Manage Team process.
- **C Work performance data**
Incorrect. Work performance data is not an input to managing the team. The Direct and
Manage Project Work process generates work performance data as an output, for a
Monitoring and Controlling process to analyze and produce work performance
information.
- **D Change requests**
Incorrect. Change requests are outputs of the Manage Team process, not an input. Change
requests are inputs to the Perform Integrated Change Control process.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 347-348

Question 165 of 210
Question ID: 651595
The Control Quality process has six tools and techniques, including:
● Data gathering
● Data analysis
● Inspection
● Data representation
● Meetings
Which of the following tools and techniques is missing from the list?
Top of Form
- **A Statistical sampling**

---

- **B Root cause analysis**
- **C Testing/product evaluations**
- **D Control charts**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The Control Quality process verifies the deliverables meet the quality requirements.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Control Quality is the process of monitoring and recording results of executing the quality
management activities to assess performance and ensure the project outputs are complete,
correct, and meet customer expectations. This process has the following six tools and techniques:
● Data gathering (e.g., statistical sampling)
● Data analysis (e.g., root cause analysis)
● Inspection
● Testing/product evaluations
● Data representation (e.g., control charts)
● Meetings

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Statistical sampling**
Incorrect. Statistical sampling is an example of a data gathering tool and technique, which
is included in the list in the question. Therefore, statistical sampling is not the missing tool
and technique.
- **B Root cause analysis**
Incorrect. Root cause analysis is a data analysis tool and technique used in the Control
Quality process. Since data analysis is in the list in the question, this answer is not correct.
- **C Testing/product evaluations**
Correct. Testing is a systematic investigation conducted to provide information about the
quality of the product or service resulting from the project. The intent of testing is to find

---

nonconformance problems in the product or service. 'Testing/product evaluations' is one of
the tools and techniques used in the Control Quality process. It is missing from the list in
the question. Therefore, this option is the correct answer.
- **D Control charts**
Incorrect. Control charts are included in the data representation tool and technique.
Therefore, control charts are not the missing tool and technique.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 298, 303

Question 167 of 210
Question ID: 651649
Which of the following is a tool and technique used in the Monitor Risks process that compares
technical accomplishments during project execution to the schedule of technical achievement?
Top of Form

---

- **A Risk audits**
- **B Reserve analysis**
- **C Technical performance analysis**
- **D Alternatives analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Read the question text carefully. Which terms are unique to this question?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The Monitor Risks process has the following three tools and techniques:
● Data analysis (including technical performance analysis and reserve analysis)
● Audits (e.g., risk audits)
● Meetings (e.g., risk review meetings)

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk audits**
Incorrect. Risk audits are a type of audit that is used to consider the effectiveness of the risk
management process.
- **B Reserve analysis**
Incorrect. Reserve analysis is a technique used to compare the amount of reserves
remaining to the amount of risk remaining to determine if the reserves are adequate.
- **C Technical performance analysis**
Correct. Technical performance analysis is a data analysis technique employed during the
Monitor Risks process that compares technical accomplishments during project execution
to the schedule of technical achievement in order to compare actual results against targets.

---

- **D Alternatives analysis**
Incorrect. Alternatives analysis is a data analysis technique used during the Plan Risk
Responses process to make simple comparisons of the characteristics and requirements of
alternative risk response options.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 453, 456

Question 168 of 210
Question ID: 651532
What type of information is not needed in order to determine the budget?
Top of Form
- **A Supporting details including basic assumptions about cost inclusions and exclusions**
- **B Information on what work packages are needed to build the project's deliverables**
- **C Project funding requirements**

---

- **D Information on planned start and finish dates for the project, and important milestones**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Consider the inputs to the Determine Budget process.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Determine Budget is the process of aggregating the estimated costs of individual activities or
work packages to establish an authorized cost baseline. The basis of estimates, project schedule
and scope baseline are inputs to the Determine Budget process. However, project funding
requirements are not.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Supporting details including basic assumptions about cost inclusions and exclusions**
Incorrect. This choice corresponds to the basis of estimates, which is an input to the
Determine Budget process.
- **B Information on what work packages are needed to build the project's deliverables**
Incorrect. This choice describes the work breakdown structure or WBS, which is part of the
scope baseline. The WBS is an input to the Determine Budget process.
- **C Project funding requirements**
Correct. Project funding requirements is an output (not an input) to the Determine Budget
process.
- **D Information on planned start and finish dates for the project, and important milestones**
Incorrect. This choice refers to the project schedule, which is an input to the Determine
Budget process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 248

PMP Exam 8 (ITTO)

Filtered Mode: Displaying 210 questions
Question 169 of 210
Question ID: 651508
Which of the following process(es) must precede the Plan Quality Management process?
Top of Form
- **A Develop Project Charter and Develop Schedule**
- **B Identify Risks**
- **C Develop Project Management Plan and Determine Budget**
- **D Identify Stakeholders and Identify Risks**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Think about the outputs of the processes and if they relate to the Plan Quality Management
process.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Plan Quality Management is the process of identifying quality requirements and/or standards for
the project and its deliverables, and documenting how the project will demonstrate compliance
with quality requirements and/or standards. This process has the following five inputs:

---

● Project charter
● Project management plan
● Project documents (e.g., stakeholder register, risk register)
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets
The stakeholder register is an output from the Identify Stakeholders process. The risk register is
an output from the Identify Risks process. Both the Identify Risks and the Identify Stakeholders
processes would need to precede the Plan Quality Management process in order to produce their
respective outputs which are inputs to the Plan Quality Management process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Develop Project Charter and Develop Schedule**
Incorrect. The Develop Project Charter process produces the project charter which is an
input to the Plan Quality Management process. However, the Develop Schedule process
does not produce any documents that are inputs to the Plan Quality Management process.
Therefore, this answer is not correct.
- **B Identify Risks**
Incorrect. The Identify Risks process results in the risk register, which is an input to the
Plan Quality Management process. However, Identify Risks is not the 'best' answer.
- **C Develop Project Management Plan and Determine Budget**
Incorrect. The project management plan is the output of the Develop Project Management
Plan process which then becomes an input to the Plan Quality Management process.
However, the Determine Budget process does not have any outputs that also serve as inputs
to the Plan Quality Management process. Therefore, this choice is not the best answer to
the question asked.
- **D Identify Stakeholders and Identify Risks**
Correct. The Identify Risks process produces the risk register, and the Identify Stakeholders
process produces the stakeholder register. Both the stakeholder and risk registers are inputs
to the Plan Quality Management process making this the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 277, 280

Question 170 of 210
Question ID: 651607
Which of the following is not an output of the Manage Team process?
Top of Form
- **A Enterprise environmental factors updates**
- **B Team performance assessments**
- **C Changes to schedule and cost baselines**
- **D Change requests**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Manage Team is the process of tracking team member performance, providing feedback,
resolving issues, and managing team changes.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**


---

Manage Team is the process of tracking team member performance, providing feedback,
resolving issues, and managing team changes to optimize project performance. This process has
the following four outputs:
● Change requests (especially preventive or corrective actions in the face of disruptive staffing
changes)
● Project management plan updates (resource management plan, schedule baseline, cost
baseline)
● Project document updates (issue log, lessons learned register, project team assignments)
● Enterprise environmental factors updates (organizational performance appraisals and personnel
skill)
Of the choices presented, only team performance assessments are not an output of the Manage
Team process, which is focused on oversight, tracking, issue resolution, and managing team
changes to optimize project performance. Instead, team performance assessments serve as an
output to the Develop Team process, which is focused on improving team competencies and
interaction, and the overall team environment to enhance project performance.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Enterprise environmental factors updates**
Incorrect. During the Manage Team process, the effects of tracking team member
performance, providing feedback, and managing team changes may require updates to
organizational performance appraisals and personnel skill that are among EEFs.
- **B Team performance assessments**
Correct. During the Develop Team process, the project management team makes formal or
informal assessments of the project team’s effectiveness in training, team building, and
colocation. These assessments are not outputs for the Manage Team process.
- **C Changes to schedule and cost baselines**
Incorrect. The Manage Team process may involve resolving issues and handling staffing
changes, which may cause the schedule to slip or the budget to be exceeded. Change
requests may be required to adjust the schedule and budget baselines, which are
components of the project management plan that may be updated as an output of this
process.
- **D Change requests**

---

Incorrect. When corrective or preventive actions are necessary to manage team changes
and resolve issues, you may initiate change requests, which explicitly listed as an output for
the Manage Team process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 350-351

Question 171 of 210
Question ID: 651522
Which of the following information, which may include the interpretation of S-curves, tornado
diagrams, and criticality analysis, is directly used to estimate the cost and time contingency
reserves?
Top of Form
- **A Risk urgency assessment**
- **B Probability distribution**
- **C Probabilistic analysis of the project**

---

- **D Probability and impact assessment**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which information is quantitative and used to make project document updates?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The cost and time contingency reserves are calculated based on the quantitative risk analysis and
the stakeholder risk tolerances to bring the risk of overrunning the project objectives to the
acceptable level. Probabilistic analysis of the project is often expressed as a cumulative
distribution of the estimation of project cost or schedule value with their associated probabilities
that could help to calculate the contingency reserve to increase the probability of project success.
While other information such as risk urgency assessment and probability and impact assessment
only help to prioritize and guide for risk responses.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk urgency assessment**
Incorrect. Risk urgency assessment is used to identify which risks require near-term
responses. It is often combined with risk rating to give the final risk severity rating. It
cannot be used directly to estimate the contingency reserves.
- **B Probability distribution**
Incorrect. Probability distribution represents the uncertainty in values such as durations or
costs and often used in project modeling and simulation to generate the probability
distribution, which could be used in estimate the contingency reserve, so it cannot be
directly used to determine the contingency reserves.
- **C Probabilistic analysis of the project**
Correct. Probabilistic analysis of the project is a result of quantitative risk analysis that
represents the cumulative distribution of project parameters such as cost or schedule with
their probabilities of occurrence. Based on that, the project team could determine the
contingency reserve for the project to achieve the project target.
- **D Probability and impact assessment**

---

Incorrect. Probability and impact assessment is used to assess and rank risks based on
qualitative analysis. It cannot be directly used to calculate the contingency reserves for the
project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 436
Bottom of Form

Question 172 of 210
Question ID: 651692
Which tool and technique used in the Identify Stakeholders process includes methods such as the
stakeholder cube, the salience model, and the power/interest grid?
Top of Form
- **A Stakeholder analysis**
- **B Stakeholder register**
- **C Stakeholder mapping/representation**
- **D Brainstorming**

---

Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which option has primarily data display functionality?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Identify Stakeholders is the process of identifying project stakeholders regularly and analyzing
and documenting relevant information regarding their interests, involvement, interdependencies,
influence, and potential impact on project success. The Identify Stakeholders process has five
tools and techniques:
● Expert judgment
● Data gathering
● Data analysis
● Data representation (e.g., stakeholder mapping/representation)
● Meetings

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Stakeholder analysis**
Incorrect. Stakeholder analysis is a data analysis technique that is used in the Identify
Stakeholders process. This analysis results in a list of stakeholders and relevant
information such as their positions in the organization, roles on the project, "stakes",
expectations, attitudes, and level of interest. It does not include methods such as the
stakeholder cube, the salience model, and the power/interest grid.
- **B Stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The stakeholder register is a project document, not a tool and technique.
- **C Stakeholder mapping/representation**
Correct. Stakeholder mapping/representation is a data representation technique and a
method of categorizing stakeholders using various methods including the stakeholder cube,
the salience model, and the power/interest grid.
- **D Brainstorming**
Incorrect. Brainstorming is a data gathering technique used to identify stakeholders that
elicits input from groups such as team members or subject matter experts. It does not

---

include methods such as the stakeholder cube, the salience model, and the power/interest
grid.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 507, 512-513

Question 173 of 210
Question ID: 651521
What is an output of the Control Schedule process that is an input to the Monitor and Control
Project Work process?
Top of Form
- **A Work performance data**
- **B Schedule baseline**
- **C Work performance reports**
- **D Work performance information**

---

Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The correct answer is an output from most of the processes that belong to the Monitoring and
Controlling Process Group.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The Control Schedule process is where the status of the project is monitored to update the project
schedule and manage changes to the schedule baseline. The Control Schedule process has the
following five outputs:
● Work performance information
● Schedule forecasts
● Change requests
● Project management plan updates
● Project document updates

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Work performance data**
Incorrect. Work performance data is the data that is not summarized or raw data that is
created during project execution. Work performance data are often used as inputs to, rather
than outputs from, control processes such as the Control Schedule process.
- **B Schedule baseline**
Incorrect. The schedule baseline is an output of the Develop Schedule process, not the
Control Schedule process.
- **C Work performance reports**
Incorrect. Work performance reports are the electronic or physical representation of work
performance information and are outputs from the Monitor and Control Project Work
process, not inputs.
- **D Work performance information**
Correct. Work performance information is a summarized or analyzed version of work
performance data. Most processes in the Monitoring and Controlling Process Group have

---

work performance information as outputs, where it then becomes inputs to the Monitor and
Control Project Work process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 222-223, 228

Question 174 of 210
Question ID: 651543
Which of the following is an output of the Direct and Manage Project Work process?
Top of Form
- **A Project management plan**
- **B Accepted deliverables**
- **C Risk register updates**
- **D Activity list**
Question answered incorrectly

---


**Hint:**

The correct answer is considered a project document update.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The Direct and Manage Project Work process has the following seven outputs:
● Deliverables
● Work performance data
● Issue log
● Change requests
● Project management plan updates
● Project document updates (e.g., risk register update)
● Organizational process assets
Direct and Manage Project Work is the process of leading and performing the work defined in
the project management plan and implementing approved changes to achieve the project's
objectives.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project management plan**
Incorrect. Project management plan 'updates' are outputs of the Direct and Manage Project
Work process. The project management plan is an output of the Develop Project
Management Plan process.
- **B Accepted deliverables**
Incorrect. Deliverables are outputs of the Direct and Manage Project Work process.
'Accepted' deliverables are deliverables that meet the acceptance criteria and are approved
by the customer. Accepted deliverables are outputs of the Validate Scope process.
- **C Risk register updates**
Correct. New risks may be identified, and existing risks may be updated during the Direct
and Manage Project Work process leading to a risk register update.
- **D Activity list**

---

Incorrect. An activity list 'update' is an output of the Direct and Manage Project Work
process as part of the project document updates. The activity list is an output of the Define
Activities process.

Question ID: 651670
Which of the following is a tool or technique used in the Monitor and Control Project Work
process?
Top of Form
- **A Cost-benefit analysis**
- **B Feedback**
- **C Cause-and-effect diagrams**
- **D Inspection**

---

Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The correct answer provides one means for determining which corrective or preventive action to
use.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The Monitor and Control Project Work process has the following four tools and techniques:
● Expert judgment
● Data analysis (e.g., cost-benefit analysis)
● Decision making
● Meetings
Monitor and Control Project Work is the process of tracking, reviewing, and reporting overall
progress to meet the performance objectives defined in the project management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Cost-benefit analysis**
Correct. Cost-benefit analysis is an example of the data analysis tool and technique used in
the Monitor and Control Project Work process. Cost-benefit analysis helps to determine the
best corrective action in terms of cost in case of project deviations. Therefore, cost-benefit
analysis is the correct answer to the question asked.
- **B Feedback**
Incorrect. Feedback is information about reactions to communications or a situation and is
an example of the communication skills tool and technique. Feedback is not a tool or
technique used in the Monitor and Control Project Work process.
- **C Cause-and-effect diagrams**
Incorrect. Cause-and-effect diagrams are an example of the data representation tool and
technique. Cause-and-effect diagrams help to identify the root cause of a problem and are
not used in the Monitor and Control Project Work process.
- **D Inspection**

---

Incorrect. An inspection is the examination of a work product to determine if it conforms to
documented standards. Inspection is not a tool or technique used in the Monitor and
Control Project Work process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 105, 111

Question ID: 651559
The Control Scope process has four inputs, including:
● Project management plan
● Project documents
● Work performance data
Which of the following inputs is missing from the list?
Top of Form
- **A Configuration management plan**
- **B Requirements documentation**
- **C Organizational process assets**
- **D Number of change requests**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Control Scope is the process of monitoring the status of the project and product scope and
managing changes to the Scope Baseline.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Control Scope is the process of monitoring the status of the project and product scope and
managing changes to the scope baseline. The Control Scope process has the following inputs:

---

● Project management plan (especially scope management plan, requirements management plan,
change management plan, configuration management plan, scope baseline, and performance
measurement baseline)
● Project documents (especially the lessons learned register, requirements documentation, and
requirements traceability matrix)
● Work performance data (raw data from the Direct and Manage Project Work process including
the number of change requests received, the number of change requests accepted, and the
number of deliverables verified, validated, and completed)
● Organizational process assets (including scope- and control-related guidance and the monitoring
and reporting methods and templates to be used)

plan, which was an input of the Control Scope process that is already listed in the question.
- **B Requirements documentation**
Incorrect. The requirements documentation is a project document that serves as an input of
the Control Scope process. It was already listed in the question.
- **C Organizational process assets**
Correct. Organizational process assets are one of the four inputs for the Control Scope
process.
- **D Number of change requests**
Incorrect. The number of change requests is among the work performance data that serves
as an input of the Control Scope process that was already listed in the question.

Question 179 of 210
Question ID: 651554
Which of the following is not an input to the Create WBS process?
Top of Form
- **A Project scope statement**
- **B Activity list**
- **C Requirements documentation**
- **D Organizational process assets**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The work breakdown structure is a hierarchy that organizes project deliverables to ensure that the
subsequent activities carried out by the project team will achieve the project objectives and meet
stakeholder requirements.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The work breakdown structure is a hierarchy that organizes and decomposes project deliverables
to ensure that the total scope of work to be carried out by the project team will achieve the
project objectives and meet stakeholder requirements. To that end, the Create WBS process has
the following inputs:
● Project management plan

---

● Project documents (project scope statements and requirements documentation)
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets
Of the choices given, 'activity list' does not belong in the list of inputs to the Create WBS
process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project scope statement**
Incorrect. The project scope statement is an output of the immediately preceding the Define
Scope process, establishing the boundaries of the complete scope for the project to ensure
the WBS includes the work to be performed, only that work, and nothing that should be
excluded.
- **B Activity list**
Correct. The activity list is created in the Define Activities process in the Project Schedule
Management Knowledge Area. The activity list is created by decomposing the work
packages of the WBS into discrete activities. Thus, the activity list would not be an input to
the Create WBS process.
- **C Requirements documentation**
Incorrect. The requirements documentation is an output of the preceding Collect
Requirements process, providing measurable detail about how individual requirements
meet business needs for the project deliverables and therefore is a logical input to the
Create WBS process.
- **D Organizational process assets**
Incorrect. Organizational process assets such as templates for the WBS, project files from
previous projects, and lessons learned can contribute to creating a WBS for the current
project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 157

Question ID: 651636
Which of the following inputs to the Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis process provides
published risk-related material such as commercial risk databases?
Top of Form
- **A Risk register**
- **B Requirements documentation**
- **C Enterprise environmental factors**
- **D Risk management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Is this material likely to be sourced internally or externally?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis is the process of numerically analyzing the effect of
identified individual project risks and other sources of uncertainty on overall project objectives.
This process has the following four inputs:

---

● Project management plan (including the risk management plan)
● Project documents (including the risk register)
● Organizational process assets
● Enterprise environmental factors (e.g., industry studies of similar projects and published
material such as commercial risk databases)

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk register**
Incorrect. The risk register provides information on identified individual risks but is not a
commercial database.
- **B Requirements documentation**
Incorrect. The requirements documentation provides details on all of the project's
requirements but does not provide published risk-related material such as commercial
databases.
- **C Enterprise environmental factors**
Correct. Enterprise environmental factors can provide a variety of risk-related materials,
including industry studies of similar projects and published material such as commercial
risk databases.
- **D Risk management plan**
Incorrect. Although the risk management plan may provide guidance to refer to published
material such as commercial risk databases, it does not contain or provide them.

Question 181 of 210
Question ID: 651698
Which tool or technique supports comparison between the current engagement levels of
stakeholders and the desired levels required for successful project delivery?
Top of Form
- **A Stakeholder engagement assessment matrix**
- **B Assumptions and constraint analysis**
- **C Stakeholder engagement plan**
- **D Stakeholder register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Look for a comparison tool.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The stakeholder engagement assessment matrix is a data representation technique that supports
comparison between the current engagement levels of stakeholders and the desired engagement
levels required for successful project delivery. One possible classification method would describe
each stakeholder as unaware, resistant, neutral, supportive or leading. Ultimately, the gap
between the current level and the desired level helps guide the communications necessary to
effectively engage each stakeholder.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Stakeholder engagement assessment matrix**
Correct. The stakeholder engagement assessment matrix supports comparison between the
current engagement levels of stakeholders and the desired engagement levels required for
successful project delivery.
- **B Assumptions and constraint analysis**
Incorrect. Assumptions and constraint analysis explores the variety of assumptions and
constraints to determine which pose a risk to the project. This choice does not correspond
to what is described in the question.
- **C Stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. Although the stakeholder engagement plan provides key guidance on how to
engage stakeholders, it is a project document, not a tool or technique.
- **D Stakeholder register**
Incorrect. Although the stakeholder register does contain important information on each
stakeholder, it does not provide a way to compare current vs. desired levels of engagement.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 516, 521-522

Question 182 of 210
Question ID: 626026
You are developing the cost management plan.
Which of the following would you likely use as part of this process?
Top of Form
- **A To-complete performance index**
- **B Alternatives analysis**
- **C Funding limit reconciliation**
- **D Cost of quality**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which option affects how costs will be determined?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The cost management plan is the main output of the Plan Cost Management process. The cost
management plan describes how the project costs will be planned, structured, and controlled. The
data analysis tool and technique for planning cost management includes an alternatives analysis.
Alternatives analysis includes reviewing funding options such as self-funding, funding with
equity, and funding with debt. It can also include consideration of ways to acquire project
resources such as making, purchasing, renting, or leasing.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A To-complete performance index**

---

Incorrect. The to-complete performance index (TCPI) is among the tools and techniques
that can be used as part of the Control Costs process, whereas the question is talking about
the Plan Cost Management process.
- **B Alternatives analysis**
Correct. Alternatives analysis is an example of the data analysis technique that can be used
as part of the Plan Cost Management process described in the scenario.
- **C Funding limit reconciliation**
Incorrect. Funding limit reconciliation is a tool and technique of the Determine Budget
process. This tool is not used to develop the cost management plan.
- **D Cost of quality**
Incorrect. Cost of quality is a tool and technique of the Estimate Costs process. This tool is
not used in the Plan Cost Management process described in the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 238

Question 183 of 210
Question ID: 651591

---

Which of the following is an input to the Manage Quality process?
Top of Form
- **A Quality control measurements**
- **B Quality reports**
- **C Enterprise environmental factors (EEFs)**
- **D Test and evaluation documents**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Manage Quality is the process of auditing the quality requirements and the results from quality
control measurements to ensure appropriate quality standards and operational definitions are
used.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Manage Quality is the process of translating the quality management plan into executable quality
activities that incorporate the organization's quality policies into the project. This process has the
following three inputs:
● Project management plan
● Project documents (e.g., quality control measurements)
● Organizational process assets

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Quality control measurements**
Correct. Quality control measurements are used to analyze and evaluate the quality of the
processes and deliverables. Quality control measurements are an example of the project
documents that are inputs to the Manage Quality process.
- **B Quality reports**
Incorrect. Quality reports are outputs, not inputs of the Manage Quality process.

---

- **C Enterprise environmental factors (EEFs)**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not include EEFs as an input to the Manage Quality
process.
- **D Test and evaluation documents**
Incorrect. Test and evaluation documents are outputs, not inputs of the Manage Quality
process.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

Question 184 of 210
Question ID: 651682
When you create the work breakdown structure, the scope baseline is the principal output.
What is the WBS component that identifies a management control point where scope, budget,
and schedule are integrated and compared to the earned value for performance measurement?
Top of Form

---

- **A Project scope statement**
- **B Control account**
- **C Planning package**
- **D Work package**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The work breakdown structure of a project is often categorized by management control points,
which in turn serve to provide accountability as organizational procedures links that are used in
schedule management and cost management.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

When creating the work breakdown structure of a project, control accounts are often used as the
higher-level categories, which in turn have planning packages and then work packages with
unique identifiers the lowest level of the WBS. In schedule management and cost management,
these control accounts and identifiers serve as organizational procedures links that are used to
provide accountability throughout the project life cycle.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project scope statement**
Incorrect. The project scope statement is distinct from the work breakdown structure,
focusing instead on describing the project scope, major deliverables, assumptions, and
constraints in more concrete detail than what was available during initiation of the project.
- **B Control account**
Correct. A control account is precisely the management control point described in the
question. The control accounts form a code of accounts, driving the identifiers that are
assigned to each work package and providing a structure for hierarchical summation of
costs, schedule and resource information.

---

- **C Planning package**
Incorrect. A control account may include one or more planning packages, which are
essentially placeholders. A planning package may reside below the control account and
may be decomposed later (such as in rolling wave planning) to include work packages with
known work content but without detailed schedule activities.
- **D Work package**
Incorrect. The work package is the lowest level of the work breakdown structure with a
unique identifier. A control account has two or more work packages, though each work
package is associated with a single control account.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 161

Question 185 of 210
Question ID: 651512
Which of the following tools and techniques is a match for the corresponding process of the
Project Resource Management Knowledge Area?
Top of Form

---

- **A RACI charts: Plan Resource Management**
- **B Organizational theory: Acquire Resources**
- **C Colocation: Manage Team**
- **D Project management information system: Develop Team**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Read each choice carefully and think about the purpose of each process.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

- **A RACI (responsible, accountable, consult and inform) chart is an example of a responsibility**
assignment matrix. A RACI can be part of the resource management plan, ensuring that each
work package has an unambiguous owner and that all team members have a clear understanding
of their roles and responsibilities.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A RACI charts: Plan Resource Management**
Correct. A RACI (responsible, accountable, consult and inform) chart is a form of
responsibility assignment matrix. This data representation technique may be used to
document team member responsibilities for the Plan Resource Management process.
- **B Organizational theory: Acquire Resources**
Incorrect. Organizational theory is a tool of the Plan Resource Management process, not
the Acquire Resources process. Applicable organizational theories may recommend
exercising a flexible leadership style that adapts to the changes in a team’s maturity level
throughout the project life cycle.
- **C Colocation: Manage Team**
Incorrect. Placing project team members in the same physical location can enhance their
ability to perform as a team. Therefore, colocation is a tool for the Develop Team process,

---

which focuses on improving the team’s competencies and environment, not the Manage
Team process, which focuses on resolving issues and managing team changes.
- **D Project management information system: Develop Team**
Incorrect. A PMIS is a tool for Estimate Activity Resources, Manage Team, and Control
Team processes but not for developing the team.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 316-317

Question ID: 651613
Plan Communications Management has eight tools and techniques, including:
● Expert judgment
● Communication requirements analysis
● Communication technology
● Communication models
● Communication methods
● Interpersonal and team skills
● Meetings
Which of the following tools and techniques is missing from the list?

---

Top of Form
- **A Data gathering**
- **B Information management**
- **C Political awareness**
- **D Data representation**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Plan Communications Management is the process of determining the project stakeholder
information needs and defining a communication approach.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Plan Communications Management is the process of developing an appropriate approach and
plan for project communication activities based on the information needs of each stakeholder or
group, available organizational assets, and the needs of the project. This process has the
following eight tools and techniques:
● Expert judgment
● Communication requirements analysis
● Communication technology
● Communication models
● Communication methods
● Interpersonal and team skills (e.g., political awareness)
● Data representation
● Meetings

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Data gathering**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not include data gathering as a tool and technique
used in the Plan Communications Management process.

---

- **B Information management**
Incorrect. Information management is a tool and technique used within the Manage
Knowledge process to create and connect people with information. The PMBOK® Guide
does not include information management as a tool and technique used in the Plan
Communications Management process.
- **C Political awareness**
Incorrect. Political awareness is an example of an interpersonal and team skill used during
the Plan Communications Management process. Interpersonal and team skill is on the list
in the question making this an incorrect answer.
- **D Data representation**
Correct. A data representation technique that can be used in the Plan Communications
Management process includes a stakeholder engagement assessment matrix. Data
representation is missing from the list in the question; therefore, this answer is correct.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 366, 376

Question 187 of 210
Question ID: 651579

---

Which of the following is a tool or technique of the Estimate Costs process?
Top of Form
- **A Bottom-up estimating**
- **B Pareto chart**
- **C Resource requirements**
- **D Run chart**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The Estimate Costs process aids in developing an approximation of the monetary resources
needed to complete project activities.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The Estimate Costs process has the following ten tools and techniques:
● Expert judgment
● Analogous estimating
● Parametric estimating
● Bottom-up estimating
● Three-point estimates
● Alternatives analysis
● Reserve analysis
● Cost of quality
● Project management information systems
● Decision making
Estimate Costs is the process of developing an approximation of the monetary resources needed
to complete project work.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Bottom-up estimating**

---

Correct. Bottom-up estimating is one of the tools and techniques used as a method of
estimating a component of work.
- **B Pareto chart**
Incorrect. A Pareto chart is a specialized, horizontal bar chart not mentioned by the name
Pareto in the PMBOK® Guide. They are often used in quality processes. It is not a tool or
technique of the Estimate Costs process.
- **C Resource requirements**
Incorrect. Resource requirements documentation is an input to the Estimate Costs process
that is used to identify the types and quantities of resources required for each work package
or activity. It is not a tool or technique of the Estimate Costs process.
- **D Run chart**
Incorrect. A run chart is a type of control chart used to determine the stability of a process.
It is not a tool or technique of the Estimate Costs process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 243-6

Question 188 of 210
Question ID: 651686

---

Which of the following is an output of the Control Resources process?
Top of Form
- **A Team performance assessments**
- **B Work performance reports**
- **C Work performance data**
- **D Work performance information**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Remember, the Control Resources process is not in the Executing Process Group but in the
Monitoring and Controlling Process Group. What is produced as a result of the data analysis
about variances between allocated resources and their availability or utilization?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Control Resources is the process of ensuring that the physical resources assigned and allocated to
the project are available as planned, as well as monitoring the planned versus actual utilization of
resources and performing corrective action as necessary. This process has four outputs:
● Work performance information (resource utilization and availability)
● Change requests
● Project management plan updates (resource management plan, schedule baseline, cost
baseline)
● Project document updates (assumption log, issue log, lessons learned register, physical resource
assignments, resource breakdown structure, risk register)
For the exam, understand the flow of work performance data, information, and reports. Work
performance data is an output of the Executing process, Direct and Manage Project Work.
Control Resources is one of the Monitoring and Controlling processes that analyze the data to
output work performance information. In turn, this information serves as an input to Monitor and
Control Project Work so that data analysis can produce work performance reports. These reports
feed into the Perform Integrated Change Control, Manage Team, Manage Communications, and
Monitor Risks processes.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Team performance assessments**
Incorrect. Team performance assessments serve as an output of the Develop Team process,
not the Control Resource process. As efforts such as training, team building, and colocation
are implemented, the project management team makes formal or informal assessments of
the project team’s effectiveness.
- **B Work performance reports**
Incorrect. Work performance reports are outputs of the Monitor and Control Project Work
process, not the Control Resources process.
- **C Work performance data**
Incorrect. Work performance data serve as outputs of the Direct and Manage Project Work
process, and as inputs for the Control Resources process. They are not outputs of the
Control Resources process.
- **D Work performance information**
Correct. As an output of the Control Resources process, the work performance information
describes how the project work is progressing by comparing resource requirements and
resource allocation to resource utilization across the project activities. This comparison
can show gaps in resource availability that need to be addressed.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 357-358

Question 189 of 210
Question ID: 651612
Which of the following is not an input to the Identify Stakeholders process?
Top of Form
- **A Schedule management plan**
- **B Requirements documentation**
- **C Project charter**
- **D Organizational process assets**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer has little to contribute to the Identify Stakeholders process?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Identify Stakeholders is the process of identifying project stakeholders regularly and analyzing
and documenting relevant information regarding their interests, involvement, interdependencies,
influence, and potential impact on project success. The Identify Stakeholders process has seven
inputs:
● Project charter
● Business documents
● Project management plan
● Project documents
● Agreements
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Schedule management plan**
Correct. The schedule management plan is not an input to the Identify Stakeholders
process.
- **B Requirements documentation**
Incorrect. Project documents such as the change log, issue log, and requirements
documentation provide information on new or potential stakeholders. They serve as inputs
to the Identify Stakeholders process.
- **C Project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter identifies the key stakeholder list and information about
stakeholder responsibilities. The project charter is an input to the Identify Stakeholders
process.
- **D Organizational process assets**
Incorrect. There are a variety of organizational process assets that can influence the
Identify Stakeholders process, including stakeholder register templates, stakeholder
registers from previous projects, and the lessons learned repository with information on
stakeholders from prior projects.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 507

Question ID: 651531
Which of the following documents is created in the Define Scope process and is an input to the
Sequence Activities process?
Top of Form
- **A Work breakdown structure or WBS**
- **B Project scope statement**
- **C Activity list**
- **D Scope management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which document is an output of the Define Scope process?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The Sequence Activities process has the following four inputs:
● Project management plan (e.g., scope baseline)
● Project documents
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Work breakdown structure or WBS**

---

Incorrect. While the WBS is an input to the Sequence Activities process as part of the scope
baseline, it is not an output of the Define Scope process but the Create WBS process.
- **B Project scope statement**
Correct. The project scope statement is an output of the Define Scope process and is an
input to the Sequence Activities process as part of the scope baseline. Therefore, the project
scope statement is the correct answer.
- **C Activity list**
Incorrect. The activity list is an input to the Sequence Activities process; however, the
activity list is an output of the Define Activities process, not the Define Scope process.
- **D Scope management plan**
Incorrect. The scope management plan is a component of the project management plan and
is not an input to the Sequence Activities process or an output of the Define Scope process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**

Question 191 of 210
Question ID: 651680

---

The inputs for the Define Scope process include the project management plan, project
documents, EEFs and OPAs.
What input is missing from this list?
Top of Form
- **A Project charter**
- **B Scope management plan**
- **C Assumptions log**
- **D Project scope statement template**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What information on the major deliverables, assumptions, and constraints would one likely have
shortly after the Initiating Process Group is complete, which might prove helpful in preparing a
detailed project scope statement?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Define Scope is the process of developing a detailed description of the project and product. This
process has five inputs:
● Project charter (high-level project description, product characteristics, and approval
requirements)
● Project management plan (scope management plan)
● Project documents (assumption log, requirements documentation, and risk register)
● Enterprise environmental factors (the organization's culture, infrastructure, personnel
administration and marketplace conditions)
● Organizational process assets (policies, procedures, templates for the project scope statement;
project files from previous projects; and lessons learned from previous projects)

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project charter**

---

Correct. The project charter is the only input for the Define Scope process missing from the
list in the question.
- **B Scope management plan**
Incorrect. The scope management plan is a component of the project management plan,
which was already listed as an input in the question.
- **C Assumptions log**
Incorrect. The assumption log is among the project documents, which were already listed
as an input in the question.
- **D Project scope statement template**
Incorrect. A template for the project scope statement is among the organizational process
assets, which were already listed as an input in the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 152

Question 192 of 210
Question ID: 651634

---

Which of the following is not an input to the Identify Risks process?
Top of Form
- **A Stakeholder register**
- **B Procurement documentation**
- **C Schedule management plan**
- **D Work performance information**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which choice is not related in any significant way to identifying project risks?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Identify Risks is the process of identifying individual risks as well as sources of overall risk and
documenting their characteristics. This process has the following six inputs:
● Project management plan (including the schedule management plan)
● Project documents (including the stakeholder register)
● Agreements
● Procurement documentation
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The stakeholder register is an input to the Identify Risks process. It helps to
identify which individuals or groups might participate in identifying risks, as well as
indicating who may be available to act as risk owners.
- **B Procurement documentation**

---

Incorrect. Procurement documentation is an input to the Identify Risks process.
Procurement documentation is reviewed to determine if external procurements may impact
overall project risk or introduce individual risks.
- **C Schedule management plan**
Incorrect. The schedule management plan is an input to the Identify Risks process. The
schedule management plan may identify areas that are subject to uncertainty or ambiguity.
- **D Work performance information**
Correct. Work performance information is an input to the Monitor and Control Project
Work process, but it is not an input of the Identify Risks process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 409, 410, 109

Question ID: 651669
Which of the following is an output of the Manage Project Knowledge process?
Top of Form

---

- **A Project documents updates**
- **B Enterprise environmental factors updates**
- **C Knowledge management**
- **D Lessons learned register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

One of the benefits of the Manage Project Knowledge process is to make any new knowledge
created available for the rest of the project.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The Manage Project Knowledge process is defined as the process of using existing knowledge
and creating new knowledge to achieve the project's objectives and contribute to organizational
learning. It has the following three outputs:
● Lessons learned register
● Project management plan updates
● Organizational process assets updates

**Details for Each Option:**

process.
- **B Enterprise environmental factors updates**

Knowledge process.
- **C Knowledge management**

---

Incorrect. Knowledge management is a tool and technique used during the Manage Project
Knowledge process; not an output.
- **D Lessons learned register**
Correct. The lessons learned register is created as an output of the Manage Project
Knowledge process early in the project. After that, the lessons learned register is used as an
input and updated as an output in many processes throughout the project.

Question ID: 651603
The Develop Project Team process has four inputs, including:
● Project management plan
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets
Which of the following inputs is missing from the list?

---

- **A Team performance assessments**
- **B Project team assignments**
- **C Human resource management policies**
- **D Work performance reports**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Develop Team is the process of improving the competencies, team interaction, and the overall
team environment while Manage Team is the process of tracking team member performance,
providing feedback, resolving issues, and managing team changes.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Develop Team is the process of improving competences, team member interaction, and overall
team environment to enhance project performance. This process has the following three inputs:
● Project management plan
● Project documents (lessons learned register, project schedule, project team assignments,
resource calendars, team charter)
● Enterprise environmental factors (human resource management policies, team member
competencies, and geographic distribution)

the Develop Team process.

question and, therefore, are not missing.
- **D Work performance reports**

Develop Team process.

Question ID: 651632
The risk report is an output of which process?
Top of Form
- **A Identify Risks**

---

- **B Plan Risk Management**
- **C Implement Risk Responses**
- **D Manage Communications**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which process would most of the information in a risk report come from?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The risk report presents information on overall project risks and individual risks to stakeholders.
The report is developed progressively throughout the various risk management processes but is
created during the Identify Risks process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Identify Risks**
Correct. On completion of the Identify Risks process, the risk report typically includes
information on sources of overall project risk and summary information on individual
project risks.
- **B Plan Risk Management**
Incorrect. Although the risk report format and content outline may be developed during the
Plan Risk Management process, the content for this report is primarily developed during
the Identify Risks process.
- **C Implement Risk Responses**
Incorrect. Although some information from the Implement Risk Responses process may be
included in the risk report, the majority of the content for this report is developed during
the Identify Risks process.
- **D Manage Communications**

---

Incorrect. The risk report is an input (not an output) of the Manage Communications
process.

Question 196 of 210
Question ID: 651653
Which of the following is not an output of the Plan Procurement Management process?
Top of Form
- **A Procurement statement of work (SOW)**
- **B Source selection criteria**
- **C Multicriteria decision analysis**
- **D Make-or-buy decisions**
Question answered incorrectly

---


**Hint:**

One of the answers is a tool and technique, not an output.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Plan Procurement Management is the process of documenting project procurement decisions,
specifying the approach, and identifying potential sellers. This process has the following ten
outputs:
● Procurement management plan
● Procurement strategy
● Bid documents
● Procurement statement of work
● Source selection criteria
● Make-or-buy decisions
● Independent cost estimates
● Change requests
● Project documents updates
● Organizational process assets updates

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Procurement statement of work (SOW)**
Incorrect. The procurement SOW describes the procurement item in sufficient detail to
allow prospective sellers to determine if they can provide the products, services, or results.
The procurement SOW is developed during the Plan Procurement Management process and
is, therefore, an output of the process.
- **B Source selection criteria**
Incorrect. Source selection criteria is a set of attributes desired by the buyer which a seller
is required to meet or exceed to be selected for a contract. The source selection criteria are
outputs of the Plan Procurement Management process.
- **C Multicriteria decision analysis**
Correct. Multicriteria decision analysis is a decision-making technique and is, therefore, a
tool and technique not an output.
- **D Make-or-buy decisions**

---

Incorrect. Make-or-buy decisions are outputs of Plan Procurement Management process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 466

Question ID: 651510
In which Project Schedule Management process is a milestone list created?
Top of Form
- **A Develop Schedule**
- **B Sequence Activities**
- **C Define Activities**
- **D Estimate Activity Durations**
Question answered incorrectly

---


**Hint:**

The correct answer is the same process that creates the activity list.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The Define Activities process is where one identifies and documents the specific actions to be
performed to produce the project deliverables.The Define Activities process has the following
five outputs:
● Activity list
● Activity attributes
● Milestone list
● Change requests
● Project management plan updates

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Develop Schedule**
Incorrect The Develop Schedule process is where one analyzes activity sequences,
durations, resource requirements, and schedule constraints to create the project schedule
model for project execution and monitoring and controlling. The Develop Schedule process
does not involve milestone lists.
- **B Sequence Activities**
Incorrect. The Sequence Activities process uses milestone lists developed in the Define
Activities process as inputs, not as outputs. Sequence Activities is where one identifies and
documents relationships among the project activities.
- **C Define Activities**
Correct. A milestone list is a list identifying all project milestones and is one of the outputs
of the Define Activities process.
- **D Estimate Activity Durations**
Incorrect. The Estimate Activity Durations process does not involve milestone lists. It is in
this process where one estimates the number of work periods needed to complete individual
activities with the estimated resources.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 183, 186
Bottom of Form

Question 198 of 210
Question ID: 651659
The Control Procurements process has eight inputs, including:
● Project management plan
● Project documents
● Agreements
● Procurement documentation
● Work performance data
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets
Which of the following inputs is missing from the list?
Top of Form
- **A Project charter**
- **B Project scope statement**

---

- **C Schedule baseline**
- **D Approved change requests**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Working with vendors may require modifications to the contract, the statement of work, or any of
the controlled project documents.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Conduct Procurements is the process of obtaining seller responses, selecting a seller, and
awarding a contract. The Control Procurements process has eight inputs, including:
● Project management plan
● Project documents
● Agreements
● Procurement documentation
● Approved change requests
● Work performance data
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project charter**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not include the project charter as an input to the
Control Procurements process.
- **B Project scope statement**
Incorrect. The project scope statement is part of the scope baseline, which is a component
of the project management plan. Although the PMBOK® Guide does not explicitly include
the scope statement as an input to the Control Procurements process, neither is the scope
statement excluded. However, since the scope statement is a component of the project
management plan, it is already included on the list in the question. Therefore, this answer is
incorrect.
- **C Schedule baseline**

---

Incorrect. The schedule baseline is a component of the project management plan which is
included on the list in the question.
- **D Approved change requests**
Correct. Approved change requests can include modifications to the contract or the
procurement statement of work. Approved change requests are inputs to the Control
Procurements process and are the input missing from the list in the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 492, 496

Question 199 of 210
Question ID: 651640
Which tool or technique used during the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process considers
characteristics beyond priority and impact such as urgency, dormancy, controllability, and
propinquity?
Top of Form
- **A Risk data quality assessment**

---

- **B Hierarchical charts**
- **C Risk probability and impact assessment**
- **D Assessment of other risk parameters**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This tool or technique is all about alternatives.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process focuses primarily on prioritizing risks by
assessing their probability of occurrence and their impact. However, it can also use other
characteristics based on project needs and circumstances. The 'assessment of other risk
parameters' technique is used to perform these assessments on such characteristics as urgency,
proximity, dormancy, manageability, controllability, detectability, connectivity, strategic impact,
and propinquity.
Note: Propinquity is a term typically used synonymously with proximity. However, in this
context, it refers more to closeness by kinship, e.g., that a particular risk is perceived as highly
significant in the mind of a specific stakeholder or group of stakeholders.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk data quality assessment**
Incorrect. Although risk data quality assessments are data analysis techniques used during
the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process, their purpose is not as described in the
question. Risk data quality assessments evaluate the degree to which the data about
individual project risks is accurate and reliable as a basis for qualitative risk analysis.
- **B Hierarchical charts**
Incorrect. Although a hierarchical chart is a data representation technique that is used
during the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process, what is described in the question
does not correspond with this choice. Hierarchical charts are used to display data using
more than two parameters.

---

- **C Risk probability and impact assessment**
Incorrect. Although risk probability and impact assessments are data analysis techniques
used during the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process, risk probability and impact
assessment involve the assessment of both risk and impact and does not consider other
factors. This choice does not fit in with the tool or technique described in the question.
- **D Assessment of other risk parameters**
Correct. This technique allows the project team to consider risk characteristics in addition
to probability and impact.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 419, 423
Bottom of Form

Question 200 of 210
Question ID: 651643
Which of the following is not an input to the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process?
Top of Form
- **A Risk management plan**

---

- **B Stakeholder register**
- **C Risk register**
- **D Quality management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which choice will not have any significant information to provide to this process?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis is the process of prioritizing individual project risks for
further analysis or action by assessing their probability of occurrence and impact as well as other
characteristics. This process has the following six inputs:
● Risk register
● Risk management plan
● Assumption log
● Stakeholder register
● Organizational process assets
● Enterprise environmental factors

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk management plan**
Incorrect. The risk management plan is an input of the Perform Qualitative Risk
Assessment process. It contains many critical elements needed for this process, including
roles and responsibilities for conducting risk management, budgets for risk management,
risk management schedule activities, risk categories, definitions of probability and impact,
and the probability and impact matrix.
- **B Stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The stakeholder register is an input of the Perform Qualitative Risk Assessment
process. It provides details of project stakeholders who may be nominated as risk owners.
- **C Risk register**

---

Incorrect. The risk register is an input of the Perform Qualitative Risk Assessment process.
It contains details of individual risks that will be assessed.
- **D Quality management plan**
Correct. Although the quality management plan includes a variety of risk considerations, it
is not an input of the Perform Qualitative Risk Assessment process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 419

Question 201 of 210
Question ID: 651562
Which of the following is an input to the Define Activities process?
Top of Form
- **A Activity attributes**
- **B Scope baseline**

---

- **C Requirements traceability matrix**
- **D Activity list**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Define Activities is the process of identifying the specific actions to be performed to produce the
project deliverables.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The Define Activities process has the following three inputs.
● Project management plan (e.g., scope baseline)
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Activity attributes**
Incorrect. Activity attributes extend the description of the activity by providing more
information about each activity. Activity attributes is an output of the Define Activities
process, not an input to the process.
- **B Scope baseline**
Correct. The project WBS, deliverables, constraints, and assumptions documented in the
scope baseline are considered while defining activities. Therefore, the scope baseline is an
input to the Define Activities process.
- **C Requirements traceability matrix**
Incorrect. The requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements
from their origin to the deliverables that satisfy them. The requirements traceability matrix
is not listed as an input to the Define Activities process in the PMBOK® Guide.
- **D Activity list**

---

Incorrect. The activity list is a documented tabulation of schedule activities that shows a
sufficiently detailed scope of work description, so project team members understand what
work is to be performed. The activity list is an output from, not an input to, the Define
Activities process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 183, 184

Question 202 of 210
Question ID: 651624
Which of the following is an output of the Manage Communications process?
Top of Form
- **A Budget forecasts**
- **B Project communications**
- **C Requirements documentation**
- **D Project charter**

---

Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Manage Communications is the process of creating, collecting, distributing, storing, retrieving,
and ultimate disposition of project information.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Manage Communications is the process of ensuring timely and appropriate collection, creation,
distribution, storage, retrieval, management, monitoring, and the ultimate disposition of project
information. This process has the following four outputs:
● Project communications
● Organizational process assets updates
● Project management plan updates
● Project documents updates

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Budget forecasts**
Incorrect. Budget forecasts are not included in the PMBOK® Guide as an output of the
Manage Communications process.
- **B Project communications**
Correct. Project communications artifacts may include but are not limited to performance
reports, deliverable status, schedule progress, cost incurred, presentations, and other
information required by stakeholders. Project communications are outputs of the Manage
Communications process.
- **C Requirements documentation**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not include requirements documentation among the
outputs of the Manage Communications process.
- **D Project charter**
Incorrect. The project charter is an output of the Develop Project Charter process, not the
Manage Communications process.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 379, 387

Question ID: 651589
The Plan Quality Management process has four outputs, including:
● Quality management plan
● Project management plan updates
● Project documents updates
Which of the following outputs is missing from the list?
Top of Form
- **A Process improvement plan**
- **B Organizational process assets (OPAs) updates**
- **C Enterprise environmental factors (EEFs) updates**
- **D Quality metrics**

---

Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Plan Quality Management is the process of identifying quality requirements for the project and
product and documenting how the project will demonstrate compliance.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The Plan Quality Management process has the following four outputs:
● Quality management plan
● Quality metrics
● Project management plan updates
● Project documents updates
Plan Quality Management is the process of identifying quality requirements and/or standards for
the project and its deliverables, and documenting how the project will demonstrate compliance
with quality requirements and/or standards.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Process improvement plan**
Incorrect. The process improvement plan is not described in the PMBOK® Guide.
- **B Organizational process assets (OPAs) updates**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not include OPAs updates as outputs of the Plan
Quality Management process.
- **C Enterprise environmental factors (EEFs) updates**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not include EEFs updates as outputs of the Plan
Quality Management process.
- **D Quality metrics**
Correct. The quality metrics describe which project or product attributes will be measured
and how compliance will be verified. Quality metrics are outputs from the Plan Quality
Management process.

**Reference:**
