Question ID: 651617
Which of the following is a tool and technique of the Monitor Communications process?
Top of Form
- **A Strategies for threats**
- **B Performance reviews**
- **C Project management information systems**
- **D Contingent response strategies**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Communications are typically delivered electronically.
Correct Answer: C

---


**Explanation:**

The Monitor Communications process has the following five tools and techniques:
● Expert Judgment
● Project management information systems
● Data analysis
● Interpersonal and team skills
● Meetings

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Strategies for threats**
Incorrect. Strategies for threats are part of the tools and techniques used in the Plan Risk
Responses process, not the Monitor Communications process.
- **B Performance reviews**
Incorrect. Performance reviews are a technique that is used to measure, compare, and
analyze actual performance of work in progress on the project against the baseline. The
PMBOK® Guide does not include performance reviews as a tool and technique in the
Monitor Communications process.
- **C Project management information systems**
Correct. A project management information system is a tool and technique used in the
Monitor Communications process.
- **D Contingent response strategies**
Incorrect. 'Contingent response strategies' is a type of tool and technique used in the Plan
Risk Responses process, not the Monitor Communications process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 388, 392

Question 205 of 210
Question ID: 651673
The Plan Schedule Management process has four inputs:
● Project management plan
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets
Which of the following inputs is missing from the list?
Top of Form
- **A Scope management plan**
- **B Project charter**
- **C Development approach**
- **D Project documents**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The missing document contains summary schedule information.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**


---

The Plan Schedule Management process has four inputs:
● Project charter
● Project management plan
● Enterprise environmental factors
● Organizational process assets

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Scope management plan**
Incorrect. The scope management plan describes how the scope will be defined and
developed, which will provide information on how the schedule will be developed. The
scope management plan is a component of the project management plan which is included
on the list in the question. Therefore, scope management plan is not the correct answer to
the question asked.
- **B Project charter**
Correct. The project charter defines the summary milestone schedule that will influence the
management of the project schedule and is the input missing from the list in the question.
Therefore, project charter is the correct answer.
- **C Development approach**
Incorrect. The development approach is a component of the project management plan that
will help define the scheduling approach, estimating techniques, scheduling tools, and
techniques for controlling the schedule. Since the development approach is a subsidiary of
the project management plan, and the project management plan is on the list in the
question, the development approach is not the missing input.
- **D Project documents**
Incorrect. The PMBOK® Guide does not list project documents as an input to the Plan
Schedule Management Plan process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 179, 180

Question 206 of 210
Question ID: 651553
The Define Scope has five tools and techniques, including:
● Expert judgment
● Data analysis
● Decision making
● Interpersonal and team skills
Which of the following tools and techniques is missing from the list?
Top of Form
- **A Focus groups**
- **B Observations**
- **C Negotiation**
- **D Product analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Define Scope is the process of developing a detailed description of the project and product.

---

Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Define Scope is the process of developing a detailed description of the project and product. It has
the following five tools and techniques:
● Expert judgment
● Data analysis (alternatives analysis)
● Decision making (multicriteria decision analysis)
● Interpersonal and team skills (facilitation of expert workshops)
● Product analysis (product breakdown, requirements analysis, systems analysis, systems
engineering, value analysis and value engineering)

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Focus groups**
Incorrect. Focus groups are among the data gathering techniques for the Collect
Requirements process, but the purpose of the Define Scope process is not to collect data,
but to analyze it and determine the boundaries and acceptance criteria for the product,
service, or result to be delivered at the end of the project.
- **B Observations**
Incorrect. The raw observations during the execution of the project form the basis for work
performance data, which is an output of the Direct and Manage Project Work process.
Otherwise, ‘observations’ do not serve as a tool and technique for any process.
- **C Negotiation**
Incorrect. Negotiation is an interpersonal and team skill first used in the Acquire Resources
process, as well as the Develop Team, Manage Team, Conduct Procurements and Monitor
Stakeholder Engagement processes.
- **D Product analysis**
Correct. Product analysis is only used as a tool and technique for the Define Scope process.
Product analysis involves translating high-level descriptions into meaningful deliverables
at a level of detail needed to design the final product or service.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 153, 693
Bottom of Form

Question 207 of 210
Question ID: 651696
Which of the following is an input of both the Monitor Stakeholder Engagement process and the
Identify Stakeholders process?
Top of Form
- **A Project charter**
- **B Stakeholder analysis**
- **C Work performance data**
- **D Issue log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The correct answer is a very basic choice and is an input to many project management processes.
Correct Answer: D

---


**Explanation:**

The issue log is an input to the Identify Stakeholders process, where it provides information on
issues that may introduce new stakeholders to the project or change the participation of existing
stakeholders. The issue log is also an input to the Monitor Stakeholder engagement process,
where it provides all the known issues related to project stakeholders.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Project charter**
Incorrect. Although the project charter is an input of the Identify Stakeholders process, it is
not an input of the Monitor Stakeholder Engagement process.
- **B Stakeholder analysis**
Incorrect. Although stakeholder analysis is used in both processes, it is a tool and
technique, not an input.
- **C Work performance data**
Incorrect. Work performance data is an input of the Monitor Stakeholder Engagement
process but is not an input of the Identify Stakeholders process.
- **D Issue log**
Correct. The issue log is an input of both processes.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 510, 532

Question 208 of 210
Question ID: 651609
Which of the following is not a tool or technique for the Manage Team process?
Top of Form
- **A Emotional intelligence**
- **B Project management information system (PMIS)**
- **C Leadership**
- **D Multicriteria decision analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Remember, you are looking for a choice that is not a tool or technique of the Manage Team
process of tracking team member performance, providing feedback, resolving issues, and
managing changes to optimize project performance.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Manage Team is the process of tracking team member performance, providing feedback,
resolving issues, and managing team changes to optimize project performance. The Manage
Team process has the following two tools and techniques:
● Interpersonal and team skills (conflict management, decision making, emotional intelligence,
influencing and leadership)
● Project management information system (resource management or scheduling software)
In the context of team management, decision making is considered an interpersonal and team
skill, particularly involving the ability to negotiate and influence the organization and the project
management team to stimulate creativity, account for risk, and focus on the project goals to be
served. In the context of acquiring resources, multicriteria decision analysis is a

---

decision-making technique using a decision matrix to systematically evaluate several
characteristics (such as availability, cost, features, experience, knowledge, skills) shared among
the choices and then rank the choices by the resulting mathematical scores.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Emotional intelligence**
Incorrect. Emotional intelligence is one of the interpersonal and team skills that serve as
tools and techniques for managing the team.
- **B Project management information system (PMIS)**
Incorrect. The PMIS is a tool for managing the team.
- **C Leadership**
Incorrect. Leadership is one of the interpersonal and team skills that serve as tools and
techniques for managing the team.
- **D Multicriteria decision analysis**
Correct. Multicriteria decision analysis is a decision-making technique used in the Acquire
Resources process, not the Manage Team process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 348-350, 332

Question 209 of 210
Question ID: 651633
Updates to which of the following are not an output of the Implement Risk Responses process?
Top of Form
- **A Issue log**
- **B Work performance information**
- **C Project team assignments**
- **D Risk report**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which option is not related to risk response implementation?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Implement Risk Responses is the process of implementing agreed-upon risk response plans. The
process has two outputs:
● Change requests
● Project documents updates (including the issue log, the lessons learned register, project team
assignments, the risk register, and the risk report)

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Issue log**
Incorrect. Updates to the issue log is an output of the Implement Risk Responses process.
Risk response issues identified during the process are recorded in the log.

---

- **B Work performance information**
Correct. Work performance information is an output of processes in the Monitoring and
Controlling Process Group including Monitor Risks. Work performance information is not
updated as an output of the Implement Risk Responses process, making this choice the best
answer to the question asked.
- **C Project team assignments**
Incorrect. Updates to project team assignments are outputs of the Implement Risk
Responses process, where suitably qualified and experienced personnel are assigned to
execute the agreed-upon risk response actions.
- **D Risk report**
Incorrect. The risk report is updated as an output of the Implement Risk Responses process,
incorporating any changes to the previously agreed risk response to overall project risk
exposure.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 449, 457

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 8 (ITTO)
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 210 questions
Question 210 of 210
Question ID: 651671

---

Which of the following is a tool or technique used in the Close Project or Phase process?
Top of Form
- **A Claims administration**
- **B Data analysis**
- **C Decision-making**
- **D Multicriteria decision analysis**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This tool and technique can be used to improve future projects.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The Close Project or Phase process has the following three tools and techniques:
● Expert judgment
● Data analysis
● Meetings
Close Project or Phase is the process of finalizing all activities for the project, phase, or contract.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Claims administration**
Incorrect. Claims administration is the process of trying to resolve any contested charges
with a vendor. Claims administration is not a tool or technique used in the Close Project or
Phase process.
- **B Data analysis**
Correct. Data analysis techniques are used to organize, assess, and evaluate data and
information. Document analysis, regression analysis, trend analysis, and variance analysis

---

are some examples of the data analysis tool and technique used in the Close Project or
Phase process.
- **C Decision-making**
Incorrect. Decision-making is a group of techniques that can be used to assist with
selecting a single choice when presented with many. Decision-making is not a tool or
technique used in the Close Project or Phase process.
- **D Multicriteria decision analysis**
Incorrect. Multicriteria decision analysis utilizes a decision matrix to provide a systematic
analytical approach to decision-making. Multicriteria decision analysis is not a tool or
technique used in the Close Project or Phase process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 121, 126
